03/01/2025, 3:59 pm - GP: The STARE (Structured Analysis of the Retina) dataset was initiated in 1975 by Dr. Michael Goldbaum at the University of California, San Diego, as part of a project funded by the U.S. National Institutes of Health.  The dataset comprises approximately 400 raw retinal images, with 20 of these images commonly used for tasks like retinal vessel segmentation.  Each image has a resolution of 700×605 pixels, and two sets of ground-truth vessel annotations are available, provided by experts Adam Hoover and Valentina Kouznetsova.  The dataset also includes expert annotations of various manifestations visible in each image, totaling 44 possible features that were reduced to 39 during encoding.  Additionally, there are artery/vein labelings for 10 images and optic nerve detection data for 80 images with ground truth.  The STARE dataset is widely used in medical image analysis research, particularly for developing and evaluating algorithms for retinal vessel segmentation and related tasks.

15/01/2025, 8:12 pm - GP: ABSTRACT
Every year, roughly hundreds of criminals are managing to break away from the surveillance.
The above incidents might pose increased dangers to public safety, and they would also give
rise to a few issues related to distrust among public servants and the public. With a challenge
posed in prison escape all the time, our project attempts to provide an easier way of catching
apprehended criminals. Our idea is the handcuffs equipped with GPS and vibration sensors
attached to the criminals while in custody and these are used to track the criminal’s activity
and give real-time data to the officials. By using GPS technology, we can trace the movement
of the criminals. These handcuffs also contain vibration sensors which alert the officials if
the criminal tries to break the handcuffs in an unethical way. The main aim is to provide
technology that can catch the criminals. Using technology, we could make the process more
efficient when compared with the traditional methods that the cops use now. Our gadget
aims to improve the searching technique that reduces the efforts of manpower and is also time
efficient. Durability and ease of tracking the criminal’s movements are at the forefront of our
design considerations. We are committed to creating a gadget that is durable, lightweight,
and comfortable for the culprits to wear and make it a robust device. These smart handcuffs
are the same as the normal ones, but they contain GPS. A GPS sensor is installed in the
handcuffs, which reads and carries the movement of the criminal in the form of data to the
satellite. The satellite changes this into real-time data and sends it to the system. It can
monitor the movement of a criminal, which may be taken as a kind of surveillance. But it’s
not just about making things work; it’s about making things work well. We are ensuring
that our gadget is comfortable to use and also comfortable to wear with fewer or no technical
errors. Our project is not just about creating an IOT device but about making a difference
in the law enforcement system as it is needed the most.
Keywords: Smart Handcuffs, GPS Tracking, Vibration Sensors, Real-Time Location, Criminal Monitoring.
15/01/2025, 8:13 pm - GP: INTRODUCTION
Prison breakouts and penetration of criminal surveillance are some of the most dangerous
threats to public safety and social confidence in law enforcement. Each year, thousands of
prisoners who escape increase the danger level for citizens and make people feel insecure in
their communities. This not only jeopardizes public safety but also strains the relationship
between law enforcement officials and the public. The ongoing challenge of prison breakouts
and criminal surveillance penetration needs to be addressed. Challenges call for novel solutions that enhance the efficiency of criminal tracking with resource optimization in policing.
To this end, our proposal under the current project develops Smart Handcuffs cutting-edge
IoT device for the police to revolutionize the management of apprehended persons. The new
idea combines state-of-the-art technologies like GPS tracking and vibration sensors into a
wearable device to ensure that surveillance is always in place with real-time updates about
a criminal’s movements.
The GPS technology integrated into the smart handcuffs allows authorities to track exactly where the person under detention is, transmitting data in real-time through satellite
to a secure system. The vibration sensors will also pick up any tampering or breaking of
the handcuffs, which will immediately alert the authorities. This way, any unethical activity
will be flagged in real-time so that quick intervention. Our approach aims to transform traditional monitoring methods by providing a durable, lightweight, and comfortable-to-wear
device that not only reduces reliance on extensive manpower but also accelerates response
times during emergencies. By focusing on durability and robust design, we aim to ensure
consistent performance with minimal technical errors, making this device reliable for longterm use. The Smart Handcuffs The project is more than just an IoT innovation. It is a
step towards the creation of a safer society, equipping law enforcement with tools that are
efficient, accurate, and technologically advanced. By using real-time data and smart alert
mechanisms, this project aims to enhance public safety and establish a new standard in
criminal tracking systems, reshaping the modern law enforcement landscape

15/01/2025, 8:34 pm - Syam: Each year, hundreds of criminals escape from custody, posing great threats to public safety and weakening public trust in law enforcement agencies. These escapes reveal critical vulnerabilities in the traditional surveillance and prisoner management systems, which often rely heavily on manual monitoring, outdated technologies, and physical manpower. Due to their efficiency and resource intensiveness coupled with the high risk of human error, these conventional methods are not as effective in delivering prompt response times, as well as inability to prevent prison break. The absence of in time tracking and anti-tamper mechanisms makes it worse because criminals get an opportunity to identify weaknesses in the restraint method and escape. Such incidents not only endanger the lives of citizens but also burden law enforcement resources because an extensive search has to be carried out to catch the fugitives. In light of these persistent challenges, there is a pressing need for innovative, technology-driven solutions that can provide continuous, reliable monitoring of detainees, enhance response times, and reinforce the overall security framework to prevent future escapes and restore confidence in the justice system.

16/01/2025, 10:13 am - GP: Each year, hundreds of criminals escape from custody, posing great threats to public safety and building trust issues between people and law enforcement authorities. These escapes reveal dilemmas in the traditional surveillance and prisoner management systems, which often rely heavily on manual monitoring, outdated technologies, and physical manpower. Due to their efficiency and resource intensiveness tripled up with the high risk of human error, these conventional methods are not as effective in delivering prompt response time, as well as inability to prevent prison break. The absence of time efficient tracking mechanisms and anti-tamper mechanisms makes it worse because criminals get an opportunity to identify weaknesses in this conventional method and escape. Such incidents not only endanger the lives of citizens but also becomes a burden for law enforcement resources because an extensive search has to be carried out to catch the fugitives. In light of these persistent challenges, there is a pressing need for innovative, technology-driven solutions that can provide continuous, reliable monitoring of detainees, enhance response times, and reinforce the overall security framework to prevent future escapes and restore confidence in the justice system.

16/01/2025, 11:32 am - GP: *CONCLUSION*
GPS-enabled handcuffs mark a huge milestone in overcoming the problems associated with prisoner monitoring and management in the contemporary police service. The suggested solution involves an integration of state-of-the-art technologies such as the SIM800 module, ESP8266 Wi-Fi module, Neo-7M GPS module, and a compact 3.7V power source to ensure the safety, efficiency, and effectiveness of the tracking mechanism. These smart handcuffs will provide a dedicated application for real-time location monitoring, enabling the law enforcement authority to monitor detainees continuously.

Incorporation of a tamper or escape attempt through a vibration sensor provides a critical layer of security. In such scenarios, the system sends an alert via the SIM800 module to the preconfigured number immediately. This advance notification system is not only minimizing response times but also ensuring authorities can act before a possible escape. The application interface will facilitate the easy access to the live location of the fugitive, and this will minimize the search burden on law enforcement resources.

Compared to traditional prisoner management methods that rely heavily on manual monitoring and outdated systems, GPS handcuffs offer a more efficient and resource-friendly alternative. These smart handcuffs leverage IoT technologies and real-time communication to address the high risks of human error and resource-intensive operations associated with conventional approaches. Moreover, the robust anti-tamper mechanism and real-time tracking capabilities restore public confidence in the justice system by enhancing the overall security framework.

This innovative approach is likely to transform the management of detainees by discouraging them from escaping, cutting the operational cost of running a jail, and providing much more efficient public safety. Further improvement could be seen through the addition of more sensors in the handcuff, enhancing battery life, and increasing system scalability as technology keeps advancing.

In conclusion, the introduction of GPS-enabled handcuffs is the practical and necessary step forward to modernize the law enforcement practice. Combining cutting-edge technology with usability in real-world applications, the solution not only addresses the shortfalls of the traditional systems but also sets a precedent for future developments in criminal monitoring and management.

16/01/2025, 12:15 pm - Syam: As illustrated in Fig 2, the data flow in the system follows a well-defined sequence of operations to ensure smooth functionality. The process starts with the product detection camera, which continuously captures images of the items in the trolley. These images are then processed by the YOLOv8n object detection algorithm running on the Raspberry Pi. The system searches for a detected product, returning to the camera to take another picture if nothing is found. Once a product is detected, the system can calculate its price using a set price list on the LCD.

29/01/2025, 9:31 am - Syam: Agile ki some extra points ivi
29/01/2025, 9:37 am - Syam: ### **Generic Activities**

1. **Communication**  
   Communication is the initial and most critical activity in software development. It involves gathering requirements from stakeholders, understanding their needs, and ensuring a clear understanding of the project's goals. This activity includes conducting meetings, interviews, brainstorming sessions, and requirement elicitation to define the scope of the project effectively.

2. **Planning**  
   Planning focuses on creating a roadmap for the project. It involves defining project goals, schedules, resource allocation, and identifying potential risks. This step ensures that the development process is well-structured and that all stakeholders are aligned on the timelines, budgets, and deliverables.

3. **Modeling**  
   Modeling is the process of creating representations of the software to understand its structure and behavior. This includes developing architectural designs, data models, process workflows, and prototypes. These models help visualize the system and serve as a blueprint for implementation.

4. **Construction**  
   Construction involves the actual development of the software, including coding and testing. This activity ensures that the software meets the specified requirements and functions as intended. It includes writing code, conducting unit and integration testing, and debugging to ensure quality.

5. **Deployment**  
   Deployment focuses on delivering the software to end users and ensuring it operates smoothly in the production environment. This activity includes installing the software, configuring it for the operational environment, training users, and collecting feedback for further improvements.

---

### **Umbrella Activities**

1. **Project Tracking and Control**  
   Project tracking and control are essential to ensure that the project stays on schedule and meets its objectives. This involves monitoring progress, holding regular status meetings, generating progress reports, and addressing any deviations from the plan promptly.

2. **Risk Management**  
   Risk management involves identifying potential risks, analyzing their impact, and planning mitigation strategies. This activity ensures that the project can handle uncertainties effectively and avoid significant setbacks by preparing contingency plans.

3. **Quality Assurance**  
   Quality assurance ensures that the software meets predefined quality standards and requirements. This activity includes conducting code reviews, quality audits, and rigorous testing to identify and address defects, ensuring the final product is reliable and robust.

4. **Configuration Management**  
   Configuration management focuses on managing changes in the software and its associated artifacts. It includes version control, tracking changes, and maintaining baselines to ensure consistency and traceability throughout the development process.

5. **Process Management**  
   Process management involves defining, implementing, and refining the processes used during software development. It ensures that the development team follows a standardized approach, improving efficiency and consistency in project execution.

6. **Reviews and Audits**  
   Reviews and audits are conducted to ensure that the project adheres to its goals, standards, and requirements. These activities include design reviews, code inspections, and milestone audits to identify issues early and maintain quality.

7. **Documentation**  
   Documentation is an ongoing activity that involves maintaining detailed records of all project activities, decisions, and software artifacts. This includes creating requirement documents, user manuals, and technical guides to support development and future maintenance.

8. **Measurement and Metrics**  
   Measurement and metrics involve collecting and analyzing data to evaluate project progress, performance, and quality. This activity includes tracking defect density, productivity rates, and other key metrics to improve decision-making and project outcomes.

06/04/2025, 9:55 pm - GP: The key contributions of this work are summarized as follows:

We propose a novel diabetic retinopathy super-resolution framework by integrating a domain-specific feature extractor (DRNet) into the perceptual path of SRGAN, replacing the conventional VGG network.

DRNet is a custom encoder trained on the APTOS dataset, specifically tailored to extract retinal-relevant features and preserve microvascular structures during upscaling.

A comprehensive loss function is employed, including content, adversarial, SSIM, LPIPS, vessel, and DRNet perceptual losses to guide high-fidelity reconstruction.

The enhanced images generated by the proposed model are validated through classification-based diabetic retinopathy grading across multiple benchmark datasets, demonstrating improved generalization and clinical relevance.

Extensive comparisons with existing methods such as bicubic, SRCNN, SRGAN baseline, and ESRGAN establish the superiority of the proposed approach in both image quality and diagnostic performance.

06/04/2025, 11:35 pm - Syam: Key contributions of this work are:

A domain-specific feature extractor called DRNet, trained on the APTOS dataset, is introduced to capture fine-grained retinal structures relevant to DR.

The conventional VGG network used in SRGAN’s perceptual loss is replaced with DRNet to better guide the generator during image reconstruction.

A set of tailored loss functions—content, adversarial, SSIM, LPIPS, vessel-based, and DRNet-based perceptual loss—are incorporated to ensure clinically meaningful image enhancement.

The super-resolved images generated by the proposed model are evaluated for their effectiveness in improving DR grading performance across different datasets, showing improved generalization and diagnostic support.

29/06/2025, 11:35 am - GP: import sys
sys.setrecursionlimit(1 << 25)

def get_ans(n, m, cols, edges):
    from collections import defaultdict

    # Build adjacency list
    graph = defaultdict(list)
    for u, v in edges:
        graph[u].append(v)
        graph[v].append(u)

    usefulness_sum = 0

    def dfs(u, parent):
        nonlocal usefulness_sum
        subtree_nodes = [u]  # Include self

        for v in graph[u]:
            if v != parent:
                child_subtree = dfs(v, u)
                subtree_nodes.extend(child_subtree)

        # Count v in subtree_nodes such that u % v == 0
        count = sum(1 for v in subtree_nodes if u % v == 0)
        usefulness_sum += count

        return subtree_nodes

    dfs(1, -1)
    return usefulness_sum

29/06/2025, 12:01 pm - GP: def GetAnswer(N, M, S, T):
    S = S.strip()
    T = T.strip()
    n, m = len(S), len(T)

    max_len = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if S[i] != T[0]:
            continue
        j, k = i, 0

        # try to match T as a subsequence starting from i
        while j < n and k < m:
            if S[j] == T[k]:
                k += 1
            j += 1

        if k == m:
            # T ends at position j-1
            # now find last match position backwards
            end = j - 1
            k = m - 1
            j = end
            while j >= i:
                if S[j] == T[k]:
                    k -= 1
                if k < 0:
                    break
                j -= 1
            start = j

            # valid T found from S[start] to S[end]
            # extend K by adding rest of the characters from S before start and after end
            left = start  # 0 to start-1
            right = n - (end + 1)
            total_len = left + m + right
            max_len = max(max_len, total_len)

    return max_len
